============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK24)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A**c2 + c3*_f*A**c4
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (of feature variable **A** only; no **t** dependence):
\[
f(A)=0.6338994126\,A^{1/3}-0.2013223514\,A^{1/2}-0.2013223514\,A^{2}.
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (by choosing its free constants) to produce **exactly three power terms** \(A^{2}, A^{1/2}, A^{1/3}\) with those coefficients, and **no other functional forms** (no logs/exp/sin/Max/Abs artifacts, no extra powers, no constants), and also must be independent of \(t\).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether its functional “basis” can be tuned to exactly \(\{A^2, A^{1/2}, A^{1/3}\}\).

---

### 1. \(A^2c0 + A^2c1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\)
Can make \(A^{c2}\) be \(A^{1/3}\) or \(A^{1/2}\), but only **one** free power term plus \(A^2\) plus constant. Cannot produce **both** \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\) simultaneously. ❌

### 2. Same as (1) plus sinusoid term
Sin term can be zeroed (set amplitude \(c5=0\)), reducing to (1), which already cannot match. ❌

### 3. \(A^3c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + A^{c4}c5\text{Max}(0,c6+t)^{c7}+c8\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence must set \(c5=0\) (or force Max term constant, but still yields extra \(A^{c4}\) term). Then remaining terms are \(A^3, A^1, A^{c2},\) constant. No way to get both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\) and \(A^2\) with correct set. ❌

### 4. Max(0,A) polynomial + exp(Max(0,A)^(1/5))
Has exp term unless \(c3=0\). Then only \(A^2\) and \(A^1\) terms (via Max), no fractional powers \(1/3,1/2\). ❌

### 5. \(A^2\) terms + \(A\exp(A\cdot)\) + \(A\) terms + constant + \(A^{-1/5}\)
To match GT must eliminate exp and \(A^{-1/5}\) and linear terms; then left with only \(A^2\) and constant. Missing \(A^{1/3},A^{1/2}\). ❌

### 6. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(A+c3)+c4\)
Rational term yields non-polynomial behavior; cannot equal a sum of pure powers for all \(A\). Even if \(c2=0\), left with \(A^2\) and \(A\) and constant. ❌

### 7. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{Ac2} + Ac3 + A^{c4}c5 + c6\)
Can set exp term off with \(c1=0\). Then have \(A^{1/3}\), \(A^1\), \(A^{c4}\), constant. Could set \(c4=2\) to get \(A^2\), but still stuck with an \(A^1\) term unless \(c3=0\). Then we have \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^2\) and constant, but **no \(A^{1/2}\)**. ❌

### 8. Logs/exp(t)/Abs(A) logs
To remove \(t\) term set \(c4=0\). Still left with log terms; cannot become pure power sum for all \(A\) unless their coefficients are zero. If zeroed, only constant remains. ❌

### 9. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(A+c3) + Ac4 + c5\)
Same issue: rational term can’t become pure fractional powers; if removed, only \(A^2\) and \(A\) and constant. ❌

### 10. \(c0 + c1\text{Max}(0,A)^2 + c2\text{Max}(0,A)\)
Only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. No fractional powers. ❌

### 11. \(A^2(\cdots)+A(\cdot)+c4\)
Only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 12. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + c3\)
Only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 13. \(A^2(\cdots)+A(\cdot)+c4\)
Only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 14. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + A^{c4}c5 e^{Ac6} + c7\)
Must kill exp term: set \(c5=0\). Then have \(A^2\), \(A^1\), \(A^{c2}\), constant. Only one fractional power available; cannot get both \(1/3\) and \(1/2\). ❌

### 15. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(Ac3+1) + c4\)
Rational term not a pure power; if removed, only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 16. Like (5) with more linear terms
After removing exp and inverse-power, left with \(A^2\) and \(A\) and constant. ❌

### 17. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(Ac3+1)^2 + c4\)
Same rational obstruction; removing it leaves \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 18. \(A^3c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3/A^{1/3}\)
Has \(A^{-1/3}\) not \(A^{+1/3}\), and no \(A^{1/2}\). Cannot transform. ❌

### 19. Adds \(t\)-dependent Max term
To remove \(t\) dependence set that coefficient \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (15)-type with rational term; cannot match. ❌

### 20. \(c0 e^{c1\sqrt{\text{Max}(0,A)}} + c2\text{Max}(0,A) + c3\text{Max}(0,A)^{1/3} + c4\text{Max}(0,A)\)
Can kill exp by \(c0=0\). Then has \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^1\) only (linear term), no \(A^{1/2}\) or \(A^2\). ❌

### 21. Max polynomial + exp(Max^(1/5))
Kill exp by \(c3=0\). Then only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 22. \(A c0\log(Ac1+1) + A^{c2}c3 + c4\)
Log term cannot become a pure power for all \(A\) unless \(c0=0\). Then only one power term \(A^{c2}\) plus constant. Missing two required powers. ❌

### 23. \(A^2c0 + A c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4|A| + c5 + c6|A|^{c7}\)
To remove \(t\), must set \(c1=0\). Then has \(A^2\), \(|A|\), \(|A|^{c7}\), constant. Could set \(c7=1/3\) or \(1/2\), but still lacks the other fractional power and also has absolute value (non-analytic sign behavior) unless restricted domain; equivalence required for all \(A\). ❌

### 24. Similar to (23) but with \(A c4\) instead of \(|A|\)
After killing \(t\) term, has \(A^2\), \(A^1\), \(|A|^{c7}\), constant. Still only one fractional power and absolute value issue. ❌

### 25. \(A^3c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\)
Only one adjustable power plus \(A^3\) and constant. Cannot get three required powers. ❌

### 26. \(A^2(\cdots)+A(\cdots)+ A\cdot/(A+c5)+c7\)
Rational term prevents pure power sum; removing it leaves only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 27. \(A^2(\cdots)+A^{c2}c3+c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{A c7}+1)\)
Log term must be killed (\(c5=0\)). Then like (1): \(A^2\) plus one power plus constant. Missing one fractional power. ❌

### 28. \(A^3c0 + Ac1 + A c2 e^{c3 t} + A^{c4}c5 + c6\)
To remove \(t\), set \(c2=0\) (or \(c3=0\) gives constant factor but still an \(A\) term). Then have \(A^3\), \(A\), \(A^{c4}\), constant. Not GT. ❌

### 29. \(A^2c0 + c1 + c2|A|^{c3} + c4\log(c5 e^{A^{c6}c7}+1)\)
Kill log by \(c4=0\). Then \(A^2\) plus one \(|A|^{c3}\) plus constant. Only one fractional power and absolute value issue. ❌

### 30. \(A^2c0 + A c1 e^{Ac2} + A c3 + A c4 + c5|A| + c6 + c7/A^{1/5}\)
Must kill exp, \(|A|\), inverse power, linear terms to resemble GT; then only \(A^2\) and constant remain. ❌

### 31. Similar to (30) without \(|A|\)
After killing exp and inverse power and linear terms, only \(A^2\) and constant. ❌

### 32. \(A^2(\cdots)+ A c2/(A+c3) + A^{c4}c5 + c6\)
Rational term must be zeroed (\(c2=0\)). Then \(A^2\) plus one power plus constant. Missing one fractional power. ❌

### 33. \(A^2c0 + A c1/(A c2+1)^2 + c3 + c4|A|^{c5}\)
Rational term must be killed (\(c1=0\)). Then \(A^2\) plus one \(|A|^{c5}\) plus constant. Only one fractional power and absolute value issue. ❌

### 34. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2 t e^{c3 t} + c4\)
To remove \(t\), set \(c2=0\). Then only \(A^2\), \(A\), constant. ❌

### 35. \(A^3c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3 + c4 e^{c5 t}\cos(Ac6)\)
Kill \(t\)/cos term by \(c4=0\). Then only \(A^3\) plus one power plus constant. ❌

### 36. \(A^2(\cdots)+ A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)} + A c5 + c6 + c7|A|^{c8}\)
Kill \(t\) term by \(c2=0\). Then \(A^2\), \(A\), constant, and one \(|A|^{c8}\). Still missing one fractional power and absolute value issue. ❌

### 37. \(A^3c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3 + c4\log(A^{c5}c6+1)\)
Kill log by \(c4=0\). Then only \(A^3\) plus one power plus constant. ❌

### 38. \(A^{2/3}c0 + A c1 e^{Ac2} + c3 + c4/A^{1/5}\)
Kill exp and inverse power: \(c1=0, c4=0\). Then only \(A^{2/3}\) plus constant. Not GT. ❌

### 39. \(A^2c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\)
Only \(A^2\) plus one power plus constant. Cannot get both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\). ❌

### 40. \(\sqrt{A}c0 + A^{c1}c2 e^{Ac3} + c4\)
Kill exp by setting \(c2=0\) (or \(c3=0\) still leaves \(A^{c1}\) but then only one extra power). With \(c2=0\): only \(\sqrt{A}\) plus constant. With \(c3=0\): \(\sqrt{A}\) plus \(A^{c1}\) plus constant—still missing \(A^2\) and the other fractional power simultaneously. ❌

### 41. \(A^2c0 + c1 + c2|A|^{c3}\)
Only one fractional power available and absolute value issue; cannot produce both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\). ❌

### 42. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{Ac2} + A c3 e^{c4 t} + A^{c5}c6 + c7\)
Remove \(t\) by \(c3=0\). Remove exp-in-A by \(c1=0\). Then have \(A^{1/3}\), \(A^{c5}\), constant. Can set \(c5=2\) to get \(A^2\), but still no \(A^{1/2}\). ❌

### 43. \(A c0 e^{Ac1} + A c2 e^{c3 t} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{A c7}+1) + c8/A^{1/5}\)
To match GT must remove \(t\), logs, exp, inverse power → leaves at best linear/constant. No fractional powers. ❌

### 44. \(A c0\log(Ac1+1) + A^{c2}c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5\)
Logs cannot become pure powers for all \(A\) unless coefficients zero, leaving constant. ❌

### 45. \(A^2(\cdots)+ A^{c2}c3 + A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6)+c7\)
The fraction term is not a pure power for all \(A\) unless \(c5=0\), reducing to \(A^2\) + one power + constant. Missing one fractional power. ❌

### 46. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(Ac3+1) + Ac4 + c5\)
